***быстрый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстрый.html>бы́стрый</a> (811)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bystrъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быстрый.html>бы́стрый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">býstryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)быстре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)быстре́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">быстре́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fast, quick, speedy, rapid</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бытность.html>бы́тность</a> (19795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ность</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бытность.html>бы́тность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">býtnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бытность.html>бы́тности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бытность.html>бы́тности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бытность.html>бы́тностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> life, existence</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stay, sojourn of somebody in some place or in the capacity of someone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бытность.html>бы́тность</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>býtnostʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">when</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бытность.html>бы́тность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мою</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:студент.html>студе́нтом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>býtnostʹ</b> moju studéntom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">when I was a student</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***быть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> (9)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">бꙑти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*byti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bytʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>Так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tak <b>býlo</b>, tak <b>jestʹ</b> i tak <b>búdet</b> vsegdá!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">So it was, so it is, and so it will always be! [from the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Anthem_of_Russia" class="extiw" title="w:National Anthem of Russia">Hymn of the Russian Federation</a>]</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:башмак.html>башмако́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bytʹ</b> pod bašmakóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be henpecked</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Omitted in the present tense except in the third-person singular "<a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a>", which is used occasionally to express possession or definition or for emphasis. "<a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a>" is originally 3rd person singular but is now used for all persons, e.g. "<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>" - "I <i>am</i> that person". See also —.</li>
<li>Negative forms with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> feature stress on the particle in standard Russian for masculine, neuter and plural forms past tense: "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a>", "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a>", "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a>".</li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный, <a href = vnd.unilang:изолированный.html>изоли́рованное</a> спряжение, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — ∆a/c.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бычок.html>бычо́к</a> (7757)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>бык</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бычок.html>бычо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">byčók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бычок.html>бычка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бычок.html>бычки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бычок.html>бычко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>бык</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: bull calf, steer</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bullhead, miller's thumb, goby</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cigarette butt, fag-end</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ZIL-5301 light truck or related vehicle</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бюро.html>бюро́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bjuró</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)

<ol><li>office, bureau</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бяка.html>бя́ка</a> (23345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бяка.html>бя́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bjáka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бяка.html>бя́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бяка.html>бя́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бяка.html>бя́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">childish</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> no-no, something disgusting, someone unpleasent, meanie
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1956</b>,  Борис Леонидович Пастернак (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boris_Pasternak" class="extiw" title="w:Boris Pasternak">Boris Leonidovich Pasternak</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:доктор.html>До́ктор</a> Живаго</cite>, book 1, part 6, chapter 3 |  translated as Larissa Volokhonsky; Richard Pevear, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Doctor_Zhivago_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:Doctor Zhivago (novel)">Doctor Zhivago</a></cite>, 2010:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a>, са́шенька. <a href = vnd.unilang:папа.html>па́па</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подумать.html>поду́мает</a>, са́ша <a href = vnd.unilang:нехороший.html>нехоро́ший</a>, са́ша <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бяка.html>бя́ка</a></b>. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Nelʹzjá tak, Sášenʹka. Pápa podúmajet, Sáša nexoróšij, Sáša <b>bjáka</b>. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"You mustn't do that, Sashenka. <p><b>бя́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> согласовываться <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>частя́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>), 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:плохой.html>плоха́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещь.html>вещь</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:бяка.html>бя́ку</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:бяка.html>бя́ки</a></i>).

***в.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> (2)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">въ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъ(n)</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁n̥</i>, zero-grade form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁én</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_3">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">v</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(location)</i> in, at, on [+prepositional]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:театр.html>теа́тре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>v</b> teátre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He’s at (in) the theater.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(direction)</i> to, into [+accusative]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:театр.html>теа́тр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On idjót <b>v</b> teátr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He’s going to (into) the theater.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(time)</i> at, in, on [+accusative]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>v</b> tri časá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at three o’clock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>v</b> pjátnicu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on Friday</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>per
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tri ráza <b>v</b> denʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">three times per day</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a>; неизменяемое <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>Употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объе́ктом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> винительном <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> предложном п.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>Пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>словами</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:начинающийся.html>начина́ющимися</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:согласный.html>согла́сные</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вавилонский.html>вавило́нский</a> (20120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вавило́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Vavilón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>balance, scale, weighing machine
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>весы́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vesý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">more common</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́н</a> (1002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">wagon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">waggon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wagen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vagón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>railway car, coach, railway carriage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ваго́н-холоди́льник</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vagón-xolodílʹnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">refrigerator car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ваго́н-платфо́рма</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vagón-platfórma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">flatcar, gondola car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ваго́н-рестора́н</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vagón-restorán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dining car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ваго́н-цисте́рна</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vagón-cistɛ́rna/cistérna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tank car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:багажный.html>бага́жный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bagážnyj <b>vagón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">baggage car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассажирский.html>пассажи́рский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">passažírskij <b>vagón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">passenger car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спальный.html>спа́льный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">spálʹnyj <b>vagón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sleeping car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:товарный.html>това́рный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вагон.html>ваго́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">továrnyj <b>vagón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">freight car, boxcar, goods van</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ва́ж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — заважничать.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-важн-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ича</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:важный.html>ва́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vážnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
